When a follower node falls behind the leader, the system may need to send a snapshot to help the node catch up. The key components involved are: (1) **Snapshot Error Definition** (server/etcdserver/api/snap/snapshotter.go): The ErrNoSnapshot error is defined here and represents when no snapshot is available. The LoadNewestAvailable method loads the newest snapshot that matches WAL snapshot entries, which is used during recovery. (2) **Snapshot Message Handling** (server/etcdserver/api/rafthttp/http.go): The snapshotHandler.ServeHTTP method receives snapshot messages from the leader and processes them. It calls h.r.Process() which can return a writerToResponse error if snapshot availability checks fail. (3) **Raft Message Processing** (server/etcdserver/server.go): The Process method (line 706) validates incoming Raft messages and delegates to r.Step(). The snapshotIfNeededAndCompactRaftLog function manages snapshot creation and compaction based on SnapshotCatchUpEntries. (4) **Configuration** (server/config/config.go, server/embed/config.go): SnapshotCatchUpEntries is the critical configuration that determines how many entries are kept after snapshotting to allow slow followers to catch up without needing a snapshot. DefaultSnapshotCatchUpEntries is set to 5000 (server/etcdserver/server.go line 83). When a node with an old snapshot attempts to rejoin (where its snapshot index is older than the entries available for log catch-up), the system cannot provide the necessary entries to synchronize. This triggers snapshot availability validation during message processing. The snapshot availability check ensures that the follower's log can be brought into sync either through entry replication (if within SnapshotCatchUpEntries) or through snapshot transfer (if the node is too far behind).\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":5372,"cache_read_input_tokens":125630,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":5372},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"58b972cf-bd0b-42fd-a411-647efc361087","uuid":"d5e4c96d-e4f6-4536-8f6d-b71f8cf70541"}
